GT Equivalence Verification (CRK3)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_w*cos(log(A + c5))
Candidate formulas: 126

GT is the fixed function (for all real \(t,A\) in its domain \(A>-1\)):
\[
f(t,A)= -0.5475236553\,A^2\;-\;0.5475236553\,A\,e^{-0.03707904807\,t}\;+\;0.7049219911\,\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must be able to represent **simultaneously**:
1) a pure \(A^2\) term with coefficient \(-0.5475...\) (no \(t\) dependence),  
2) a term exactly of the form \((\text{const})\cdot A\cdot e^{(\text{const})t}\) with coefficient \(-0.5475...\) and exponent \(-0.037079...\),  
3) a term exactly \((\text{const})\cdot \cos(\log(A+1))\), i.e. cosine of a logarithm, not a logarithm itself, not cosine of \(A\), not cosine of \(\log(kA+1)\) unless it can be made \(\log(A+1)\).

Below, I check each candidate for whether its function class can include these three components. If a candidate lacks any needed functional form (e.g., no cosine-of-log term), it cannot match for all \(t,A\).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK3)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_w*cos(log(A + c5))
Candidates evaluated: 126
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.5475*A² - 0.5475*A*exp(-0.0371*t) + 0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `A²` (with coefficient)
2. `A*exp(αt)` (with coefficient, where α < 0)
3. `cos(log(A + 1))` (with coefficient)

Let me analyze the key structural requirement: the GT contains `cos(log(A+1))`, which is a very specific function. No polynomial, rational function, exponential, simple trigonometric, or logarithmic function can exactly reproduce `cos(log(A+1))` for all A ≥ 0.

Let me check which candidates could potentially contain `cos(log(A+1))`:

**Key insight:** `cos(log(A+1))` cannot be expressed as:
- Any polynomial or rational function of A
- `log(A*c + 1)` terms
- `exp(A*c)` terms
- `sin(A*c + d)` or `cos(A*c)` terms
- `A^c` power terms
- `|A|/(c + |A|)` terms
- Combinations of the above

The only candidates that could potentially match need to contain `cos(log(...))` or equivalent.

Let me scan for candidates with `cos(log(...))`:

- **Candidate 56:** `c5*exp(c6*cos(c7*log(c8*Abs(A*c9) + 1)))` - This has `exp(cos(log(...)))`, not `cos(log(...))`. Cannot match.
- **Candidate 68:** `c4*sin(c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8) + 1))` - This is `sin(c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8)+1))`. Note `log(c7*exp(A*c8)+1)` is a softplus, not `log(A+1)`. Cannot match.
- **Candidate 88:** `c4*sin(c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8 + c9*t) + 1))` - Similar, involves t in the log argument. Cannot match.
- **Candidate 122:** `c5*cos(c6*exp(A*c7 + c8*t))` - cos of exponential, not cos of log.
- **Candidate 123:** `c5*cos(c6*exp(A*c7))` - cos of exponential.
- **Candidate 124:** `c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8))` - exp of sin.

None of the candidates contain `cos(log(A + c))` as a basis function.

Since `cos(log(A+1))` is linearly independent from all basis functions present in any candidate (polynomials, exponentials, logarithms, trigonometric functions of A, rational functions, etc.), no candidate can exactly match the GT.

Let me verify there's no clever identity I'm missing. The function `cos(log(A+1))` can be written as `Re((A+1)^i)` where i is imaginary. This cannot be expressed as any finite combination of the basis functions present in the candidates.
